## Material Types

- M_: Base materials
- MI_: Material instances
- MF_: Material functions

## Modding Guide

### Creating Custom Materials

1. Create base material in UE5
2. Set up texture parameters
3. Configure material properties
4. Create material instances for variants
5. Apply to meshes

### Material Properties

- Base Color
- Roughness
- Metallic
- Normal Map
- Emissive
